 However, the growth in GDP for the last several years is not happening as expected
 kaise mapa jaataa he arthvyavastha kaa aakaarkisi desh kii arthvyavastha ke aakaar ko uski kul sakal gharelu utpaada (GDP) se mapa jaataa he
 That is, the total gross domestic product, the size of the economy
 sakal gharelu utpaada yani jidipi ek vittiya varsh main desh kii seemaa ke bheetar utpaadit kul vastuon or sevaaon kaa kul jod hota he
 It is considered the size of the economy and the rate of growth in it is considered as the rate of growth of the economy
 jidipi ko is tarah se maapte hai: gdp=khapat+nijee nivesh+sarkari kharch+niryaat-aayaat
 That is, after adding the consumption, private investment, government spending and exports of a country to reduce the imports from it, then it is the size of its GDP or economy

 tranjaction charge kaa yah nayaa niyam 1 march 2017 yani aaj se lagu ho gaya he
 HDFC has given 4 free transactions, then 150 rupees
 According to the new rule of HDFC, the country's largest private bank, any customer can now withdraw cash and deposit cash four times in a month
 paanchaven or uske baad ke sabhi tranjaction par bank 150 rupee pratitranjaction chargevasulegi

 vahiin aap non home branch se ek din main 25,000 rupee kii nikasi karte hai to aapse kisi tarah kaa koi charge nahin liya jayega
